< Review>
Seated quickly at an enclosed patio. Great view looking up at tall palms as whispers of clouds floated by. If you like sports, a large monitor was well placed for viewing so it's a great spot for outdoor dining in this time of COVID restrictions.
I wish the food had been better. After a loooooong wait, the crawfish gumbalaya and my alligator sausage po-boy arrived. The sausage was reminiscent of a spicy Polska Kielbasa and the roll was crisp, the sauce delicious. However, the grilled onions and peppers that were noted in the menu were missing, instead substituted with lettuce and tomato. The gumbalaya was all heat and little flavour. Our drinks? The bottle of beer was past its "best by" date and the only flavour in my Dixie Mule was that of lime- ginger beer was completely absent and I doubt there was much vodka added to that mug filled to the brim with ice. Seems like a nice place to eat, given the many people there, but unfortunately all of our choices were found to be lacking. One last thing- please fix the stall doors in the ladies bathroom! Neither has a functioning lock and one stall has at least a 3-inch gap when the door is shut.<//Review>

<user_name>Ken Peters</user_name><date>1605070536535< /date><rating>5</rating><review>2020.  We were staying in a hotel in Hermosa Beach near the Rajun Cajun in Redondo Beach, Ca, and we decided that Cajun food would be a great change of pace.

I spent seven years in the 1970‚Äôs in N.O. so I was familiar with the food served at Commander‚Äôs Palace, Tujaque‚Äôs, Antoine‚Äôs, Brennan‚Äôs and other fine dining venues in the Crescent City.  The Rajun Cajun represents their cuisine very well.

We ordered Jumbo Shrimp grilled with fresh vegetables and corn bread and the Etouffee Combo which came with red-beans-and-rice (one word in N.O.) with sausage which is traditional and ‚Äúgumbolaya‚Äù, their take on Jambalaya.

Everything was great including the fresh vegetables which were perfectly prepared.  The three elements of the Etouffee plate were quite distinct in flavor and texture despite their similarities (all over a rice base).
The dishes invoked many fond memories of my time in New Orleans and of its very distinctive cuisine.

If you have an opportunity, visit the Ragin‚Äô Cajun for a taste of the distinctive New Orleans cuisine then, visit one of my favorite cities, New Orleans, Louisiana.

Take-out, delivery, curbside and socially distanced outside dining are all provided by a socially aware management.<//review>< pictures>

1586737110299< /Time>
<rating>5< /rating>< text>
Many say Rajun Cajun is an oddity for Redondo Beach California, but I say it is a diamond in the rough. I remember going to grand opening several years ago and being awestruck by how good the Surf and Turf was. I love just about everything they have but the Surf and Turf is my favorite plus it is a safe place to start. Over the years, they have had wonderful deals and boils that are opportunity not to be passed up. When I first looked at the drink menu when I was underage and I vowed to try the fancy drinks when I turned 21. The skull drinks are creative and taste fantastic. The Diablo is my favorite. On Easter, my parents and I got the deep fried turkey dinner plus fixings and it was the best turkey I have ever had.

Now the important part. Rajun Cajun is a family owned restaurant and like every restaurant, had been hit hard by COVID-19. The family owned restaurants are the first to close for good during times like these and I along with friends and family, would be deeply saddened if Rajun Cajun closed.

If you have never been to Rajun Cajun, now is the time and if you are a fan, please support our New Orleans away from New Orleans, Rajun Cajun.<//text>

The first time we went was better, but we went on New Years day 2018 and the food came warm (not hot). The stuffing inside of the "Stuffed Red Snapper" tasted questionable...and almost had a defrost taste to it. I had to send that back because I didn't trust it.

Lastly the bignets tasted like fried tortillas sprinkled in an abundance of powder sugar...I couldn't believe they even brought that to the table.

Nice New Orleans atmosphere, but disappointed in the temperature and quality of the food.</review>

< Review>
We have gone here a few times for lunch, usually groups of 4 or 5. The food is mediocre, but its a cool atmosphere. Our last visit was rather disappointing. when it came down to the bill, I noticed it had a gratuity already included. I caught it prior to leaving cash with the receipt. As we were driving back to work, coworkers were complaining how expensive the prices had risen since last visit. I noted to them the tip was already included (on our group of 4!!) they were furious. Not only did they include the tip to the bill, it was at the 22% mark. Some of the group left additional cash not reading the invoice. It felt like we were robbed by the waitress. I'm aware that gratuity is usually included with large groups, we were a group of 4. For those that left cash tip,,.. they should have read the itemized receipt. But I think this is a poor practice and is unacceptable. We will not be back. The prices have been rising past the food quality as it was. This was enough to take it off the company lunch rotation.< /Review>

I really like their crawfish ettoufee (spelling?) and their servings are BIG!  If you want extra flavor, there are plenty of sauces you can add yourself. It's also a great place to watch sports. <UserId.>103692892444279397507<//UserId.><pics>None< /pics>< Review>
What a great birthday brunch!
I live in Central California and visit Ragin Cajun Cafe everytime I'm in the area since being introduced to this great place by my sister and brother-in-law. This past Sunday I celebrated my birthday, here, along with my entire family. It wasn't hard to convince everyone considering that the ladies in my group love the bottomless mimosas and all us guys like those abita beers.
If great food, awesome beers, and well prepared cocktails is your thing then make Ragin Cajun Cafe your next stop. If you've never had cajun cooking or it's been a while then ask to be seated at Nick's or Melissa's section. Nick will explain why you should try alligator meat and/or frogs legs in such a way that it's crazy not to order both. Melissa has such a southern hospitality that if you happen to like the skull glass where The Reaper is served in, a brand new one in a box will find it's way to your table along with a round of moonshine shots for everyone. The alligator is great the frog's legs are tender and savoury but the Stuffed Snapper, Surf and Turf, and Jambalaya are to die for. But no matter what you order as your main dish always make sure to ask Nick or Melissa what abita beer goes best with your meal.
Remember if you're near the Redondo Beach Pier don't bother wasting your money in their fast food places, take the 3 minute drive to the Ragin Cajun Cafe and enjoy the rest of your night.<//Review>

<Review>12/29/2018 . Guess what, yep had burger again. Trying to stay away from Carbs so had coleslaw with it, it really was good for plain coleslaw. I guess they decided that they needed something for the non Cajun food eaters. Me and the wife sometimes are just looking for a great burger, who thought it would be here. High quality meat and bun, WOW. I was addicted to the Shrimp Po Boy before and Cajun Chicken and Sausage Chowder. I have to admit I still am crazy about that.  I have to tell you the Brisket looked really good. Someone next to me had that and they said it was wonderful. I have to admit I've been there a couple of times before but didn't write about it. Went to the Blues Festival they had and it was fun. Look for the Crayfish Festival in April.

UPDATE:  7/29/2018. Had the steak tonight, man was that good and potato salad. Wife can't stop ordering the bisque. Finally ordered something different, then the blacken shrimp Po Boy, wasn't cheap, but steak was first class, ate everything except the plate.   Been back a number of times for Lunch, but like to update every once in a while.   UPDATE: 12/19/2017   This time I went with my wife and friend. I was sitting next to a couple and asked them about their meal. I told him I am confused about the reviews I've read. They stated that they are  from Louisiana and they tried to explain that people who aren't from Louisiana and are from California just don't understand the food correctly and that this is the only restaurant they come across out here that tastes exactly and the closest to the food they grew up with. <time>1506017439581< /time><rating>1<//rating><Text>9-17-2017. HEAVEN! HEAVEN! HEAVEN! DEJA VU ALL OVER AGAIN! Had dinner last night at the NEW LOCATION in Hermosa Beach. It is across the street from the ORIGINAL location on Peir Ave. As I walked through the door a big smile and hello from Jeanie. The place was pretty full but there was a single table open so I sat down and the server was there right away with a big smile asking for a drink order and a menu. The restaurant had the same vibe as the old place across the street. Steve came by and had that great hello and I could tell he was happy to see how things were going. Lot's of happy people enjoying a great dinner and the food and service was as great as ever! Had the Jambolaya/Gumbolaya combo, the wonderful sourdough bread and pecan pie. Mmmmmmmm! From all the folks eating there and working there it was easy to tell everyone was enjoying the night! So I guess the only thing else to say is, HALLELUJAH THE ORIGINAL IS BACK! See you next week!

THIS IS FOR THE REDONDO BEACH LOCATION ONLY. I have been wanting to write this for awhile. I have been a Ragin Cajun customer since 1998. I use to eat there almost every Thursday after our managers meeting for 10 years. Steve, Jeanie and the rest always made me feel like I was part of the family over for lunch. My favorites were the jambalaya gumbolaya combo, pork chops in brown gravy and cajun chicken salad. Even got to meet Steve & Jeanie's mom when she came out to see the Price is Right! Last time in about a month a go because I had a craving for the pork chops (combo & cheesecake cravings I got from the truck). The pork chops were dry and tough (had to use a knife!), the service slow and not good, had 2 different drinks brought to my table I did not order! Maybe the worst was no sourdough bread (a staple with Steve) but instead some godawful dry bacon cornbread. With the prices twice what they use to be, service not half as good and food not nearly as good it is no wonder the place was half empty from the old one in Hermosa on Pier Ave. I understand from the truck guys Steve no longer has anything to do with the restaurant just the trucks now. <user_name>Jeanette Rodriguez<//user_name><Time>1556979599904< /Time><Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
This is my favorite New Orleans food styled restaurant.
It's a very cozy laid back southern style home cooked meal kinda place.
It has Louisana decor and their famous jazzy blues like funk music playing in the background. It has a full sized bar, plenty of seats, booths, high top tables, great ambiance and simply delicious comfort food.
It also has my all- time must have and favorite- good ole' southern yummy SWEET TEA!!! I just can't get enough!  So Deeee-licious!!!üòã
My favorite starters are the popcorn shrimp and the garden salad and their  homemade French salad dressing.
It's really great!!!
My usual entrees are the  Gumbalaya combo, Gumbalaya, Chicken & Sausage gumbo, Red beans & rice w/ sausage. It comes without sausage for the Vegans. They also have a Veggie Vegan Gumbo which is really good too.
I just love this place!!
Anything you order, and they do have quite the assortment of choices will be absolutely fantastic!
You will not be disappointed.
They also have daily and seasonal specials on unique foods of Na'orlins like-Crawfish. Oh yeah, they have BEIGNETS!! If you have or have not been to Na'lins- these are famous!!
Soooooo gooood!!!
The owners are husband and wife. If you go as often as I do you get to see them alot. They say hello and make you feel at home, literally.
I eat here like 2-3 times a week
and love my leftovers!
They also have Happy Hour food and drinks. They serve a BOTTOMLESS (unlimited) Bloody Mary(my favorite) and Mismosa for $16.
Uhhh, just come eat for yourself!!
Enjoy! Can you tell I do?üíü‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê</review>

< Text>
If your looking to have great authentic Cajun food that tastes like it's straight from the bayou then you've found it. As a Louisiana local that moved here i'd been searching for good cajun food that tasted as good as it did back home.

This was not as easy as i thought it would be, especially given the diversity of different foods and cultures we have in Cali. And after repeated disappointments with the fake cajun restaurants here i finally found this gem.

I've been coming here and seeing the owner stephen since they had their original location in hermosa beach years ago. If your going to come down and sample some of this delicious food do yourself a favor and try the Bisque with Hush Puppies in it. And for those of you who like a drink or two this new location has a Moon Shine bar as well :-)<//Text>
